1932 ond BBC anh udaa TV broadcasting hiijee.
1920 ond anhnii huviin radio nevtruulgee tsatssan baina. in US
1897 ond Braun guai Braun tube-ee buteejee
1991 ond wordl wide web buyu WWW neegdjee. (1989-s ehelsen)
1990 onoos e-commerce hugjij ehelsen gej uzdeg um bn
1982/83 onoos TCP/IP standartchilagdsan bn
1971 ond anhnii e-mail bichigdjee.
2005 onoos Web 2.0 buyu user n web-tei interaction hiih bolomjtoi, uuruur helbel user-ud content-g n hiideg web-uud erchimtei delgerj.
2002,2003 onuudaas friendster, linkedin, myspace edr ehelsen yum bn. Gehdel fb-d bariulsan da hoorhii.
2001 onoos gar utsan deer Java app hiideg bolj. "i App"
2000 onoos utasnii shugam ashiglaj internet holbogddog DSL, ADSL service delgerchee
Baga baihad Mongold Mobicom-n wap geed uilchilgee baisansan, ter heden on yum boloo. ymar ch gsn l 1999 onoos hoish baih n.
1999ond anh udaa gar utas internet-d holbogdjee. Ter n "I mode" gedeg service baiv
1998 onoos anhnii hotspot service US-d eheljee. MobileStar
80-aad onoos information network service-uud erchimtei urgujij ehelsen um bn
OSI model ni 1977onoos hiigdej ehleed 1983 ond batlagdsan yum bn
Bidnii odoo heregledeg ethernet n 1973 ond buteegdsen yum bn
Delhiin hamgiin anhnii tomoohon computer network ARPANET n 1969 ond buteegdjee
Delhiin hamgiin anhnii hiimel daguuliin broadcast-g yoponchuud Tokyo 1964 olympics-n uyeer hiijee
Sputnik1 -s 24 jiliin daraa buyu 1981 ond Gurragchaa guai nissiin baina
1957 ond anhnii sansriin hiimel daguuliin turshilt amjilttai boljee. Ene n US-d sputnik crisis gedeg nereer aldartai Sputnik 1 hulug baiv
Anhnii telephone-n patent-g 1876 ond A.G.Bell guai avjee
Zia unuudur ICT tech-n tuuhiin talaar heden tweet hiichii

2005 onoos Web 2.0 buyu user n web-tei interaction hiih bolomjtoi, uuruur helbel user-ud content-g n hiideg web-uud erchimtei delgerj.
2002,2003 onuudaas friendster, linkedin, myspace edr ehelsen yum bn. Gehdel fb-d bariulsan da hoorhii.
2001 onoos gar utsan deer Java app hiideg bolj. "i App"
2000 onoos utasnii shugam ashiglaj internet holbogddog DSL, ADSL service delgerchee
Baga baihad Mongold Mobicom-n wap geed uilchilgee baisansan, ter heden on yum boloo. ymar ch gsn l 1999 onoos hoish baih n.
1999ond anh udaa gar utas internet-d holbogdjee. Ter n "I mode" gedeg service baiv
1998 onoos anhnii hotspot service US-d eheljee. MobileStar
80-aad onoos information network service-uud erchimtei urgujij ehelsen um bn
OSI model ni 1977onoos hiigdej ehleed 1983 ond batlagdsan yum bn
Bidnii odoo heregledeg ethernet n 1973 ond buteegdsen yum bn
Delhiin hamgiin anhnii tomoohon computer network ARPANET n 1969 ond buteegdjee
Delhiin hamgiin anhnii hiimel daguuliin broadcast-g yoponchuud Tokyo 1964 olympics-n uyeer hiijee
Sputnik1 -s 24 jiliin daraa buyu 1981 ond Gurragchaa guai nissiin baina
1957 ond anhnii sansriin hiimel daguuliin turshilt amjilttai boljee. Ene n US-d sputnik crisis gedeg nereer aldartai Sputnik 1 hulug baiv
Anhnii telephone-n patent-g 1876 ond A.G.Bell guai avjee
Zia unuudur ICT tech-n tuuhiin talaar heden tweet hiichii
